## Overall Closure Bar

- overall verdict: `still_open`
- closure bar: the rollout stays open until every source row currently marked `Open`, `Partial`, or `Contract-undefined` has row-specific implementation, tests, or exact evidence, and the source matrix records `Closed` or `Covered` for that same row id with concrete files, commands, and gate outcomes.
- row-owned truth rule: later closure work must report final truth per source row id, not only per subsystem, smoke suite, or broad group-chat area.
- residual rule: `accepted_with_explicit_follow_up` is not an acceptable final row outcome for a still-unresolved source row.
- evidence rows rule: rows classified `repo_external_proof` or `needs_repo_evidence` must not be marked closed by adjacent host tests alone; they need the named Go, raw-protocol, simulator, device-lab, relay, packet-capture, or privacy proof called out by the row.
- test-only rows rule: `needs_tests_only` rows may start by proving existing behavior, but if direct tests expose a real gap, the same row-owned session must patch that exact gap before closure.
- no unsupported rows rule: this trusted-private retained matrix contains no `unsupported_product_scope` rows; public-room semantics stay out of scope except where the row explicitly guards against accidentally exposing them.

Focused relay and node gates plus `git diff --check` passed after same-session recovery of a stale zero-peer sender fixture. Live authoritative relay group-state control-plane semantics remain separate scope. |

## Evidence Map

- Every row has a row-owned ordered-session entry below with likely code-entry files, likely direct tests or regressions, named gates, dependency notes, and closure docs.
- The original decomposition made no `covered_in_repo` claims because the retained source matrix initially had only unresolved rows; closure sections now record row-owned or prerequisite-backed `Covered` evidence for all 49 retained source rows.
- EK-003 is now recorded as `Covered` by `PREREQ-DEVICE-IDENTITY`: first-class group member device rosters, invite/admission device binding, Go envelope/config device validation, per-active-device key distribution, direct key-update source/recipient binding, offline replay device-origin binding, and fake-network valid-device versus invalid-device proof are implemented and green.
- EK-004 is now recorded as `Covered`: signed `group_offline_replay` generation/verification and all-event-family offline/pending/history replay signature-equivalence are implemented and green, while direct invite/key/audit/live-validator evidence remains preserved.
- EK-005 is now recorded as `Covered` by `PREREQ-FUTURE-EPOCH-KEY-REPAIR`: durable queue/key-sync repair primitives, retry-after-key-arrival behavior, and safe finalization are implemented and accepted by final QA.
- EK-006 is now recorded as `Covered`: raw Go proof covers epoch grace, epoch expiry, and removed/non-member previous-epoch rejection, while Flutter app-level proof covers local stale-send rejection and live/offline removed-sender cutoff behavior without normal post-cutoff UI rows.
- EK-011 is now recorded as `Covered` by `PREREQ-WELCOME-KEY-PACKAGE` final QA: first-class welcome/key-package modeling, signed payload binding, invalid-package rejection before side effects, durable replay tombstones, production local package-id wiring for listener/UI accept paths, and direct/named-gate proof exist. The prerequisite is accepted/qa_passed.
- EK-012 is now recorded as `Covered`: shipped message/invite replay, signed transition replay, future/missing-key replay, welcome-package replay/tombstones, and the remaining trusted-private remote event families now have concrete replay protection, duplicate/conflicting replay, and invalid-signature evidence from the prerequisite chain ending in `PREREQ-REMOTE-EVENT-FAMILIES`.
- OS-006 is now recorded as `Covered` and accepted by `PREREQ-HISTORY-GAP-REPAIR` final QA: durable gap lifecycle state, relay-authorized cursor gap metadata, production relay/Go/Dart repair range retrieval, deterministic range/hash validation, authorized multi-source fallback, listener/dedupe replay application, and UI repair-state proof are implemented and green.
- DB-002 is now recorded as `Covered`: migration/helper code provides a tamper-evident local group event-log hash chain with replay conflict detection and chain verification, and production wiring plus focused tests cover accepted messages, membership, metadata, roles, `key_rotated`, and direct key-update commits.
- DB-004 is now recorded as `Covered` by `PREREQ-GROUP-SYNC-RECEIPTS`: durable group sync cursor, durable group receipt storage, transaction-scoped message/receipt/read-state/cursor page apply, fail-fast normal/system replay, rollback proof, and final QA acceptance exist.
- DB-006 is now `Covered` by `PREREQ-SECRET-STORAGE-WRAPPING`: group media keys and group key material are stored in `SecureKeyStore`, ordinary SQL rows contain only deterministic `secure:` references, legacy plaintext-equivalent rows are scrubbed on startup before group-key mirroring, repository reads hydrate when material exists, and missing referenced material fails closed.
- DB-012 is now recorded as `Covered`: current repo evidence proves shipped duplicate/idempotent apply paths plus welcome-package invite tombstone, signed-transition, durable receipt idempotency, and trusted-private `member_banned`, `member_unbanned`, and remote `group_message_deleted` apply/tombstone idempotency from `PREREQ-REMOTE-EVENT-FAMILIES`.
- ER-001 is now recorded as `Covered`: invalid signatures across shipped validator event families reject and emit privacy-safe, rate-limited Go logs plus app-visible `group:validation_rejected` diagnostics that carry only hashed identifiers and bridge into Flutter diagnostics without normal group-message callback side effects.
- ER-002 is now recorded as `Covered`: unknown message and reaction senders fail before visible state or local notifications, removed-sender cutoff behavior remains enforced, and fake-network proof confirms removed-member notifications stay suppressed until rejoin.
- ER-004 is now explicitly recorded as `prerequisite-blocked`: current repo evidence proves diagnostics and safe offline unrecoverable placeholders, but the source row remains `Partial` until live and offline missing-key content have durable key-repair trigger, pending/repair/finalization lifecycle, and safe user-visible placeholder behavior.
- ER-005 is now recorded as `Covered`: shared flow-event, group diagnostic, and GoBridge error surfaces redact secret-bearing keys, raw encrypted blobs, long Peer IDs, and multiaddrs before logs, diagnostic streams, and caller-visible error responses.
- AB-006 is now recorded as `Covered`: media policy, send, listener, offline replay, and fake-network tests prove suspicious, oversized, hashless, mismatched, and tampered group media is blocked before persistence, auto-download, recipient storage, or done/display state.
- UI-003 is now recorded as `Covered`: group info and conversation surfaces show encrypted/key-epoch state, key-change text, verified-member counts, and identity/verification warnings from repository key/member/contact safety state without exposing key material, while member rows continue to show current/saved safety numbers for changed identities.
- UI-005 is now recorded as `Covered`: missing-key replay stores one generic `undecryptable` placeholder without decrypting or exposing original plaintext, and the conversation UI renders that placeholder without unsafe failed-media controls.
- SP-001 is now recorded as `Covered`: relay group inbox store/retrieve/cursor now authenticates the transport peer, rejects spoofed senders and empty recipient ACLs, persists per-message recipient ACLs, and filters replay retrieval to sender or stored recipients; existing node and relay media proof covers secure libp2p negotiation, PubSub authorization, and media ACL rejection for shipped protocol surfaces.
- SP-002 is now recorded as `Covered`: native group inbox requests no longer serialize retired plaintext push preview fields, stale Flutter retry payloads do not re-emit those fields, topics/rendezvous/logs omit human-readable group metadata, group push remains generic/data-only, and diagnostics remain sanitized; unavoidable relay-visible participation metadata is explicitly scoped.
- SP-003 is now recorded as `Covered`: focused Go and Flutter tests prove repeated shipped random artifacts are shaped correctly and do not collide across samples, including group IDs, group keys, group nonces, native and Flutter message IDs, direct invite IDs, identity entropy, and X25519 ephemeral-public-key HKDF salts/nonces; non-shipped link invite tokens and externally supplied platform push tokens are explicitly not claimed.
- EC-001 is now recorded as `Covered`: invalid pending invite accepts are directly classified and state-safe for expired, revoked, wrong-identity, malformed/tampered, and already-used cases; wrong identity now has a distinct result/snackbar, and supporting store-path tests keep delayed invalid copies from creating pending or group state.
- EC-003 is now recorded as `Covered`: future-dated messages clamp or order safely, unknown live future epochs reject before delivery, offline future epochs store one safe undecryptable placeholder, and later valid replay dependencies enrich sparse prior rows without duplicate/corrupt state; durable future-key repair remains EK-005/ER-004.
- EC-004 is now recorded as `Covered`: listener, message/reaction handler, fake-network membership, and resume-recovery evidence proves old valid events apply only within policy cutoffs and cannot roll back finalized newer metadata, membership, role, key, dissolve, local-delete, message, or reaction state.
- EC-006 is now recorded as `Covered`: current repo evidence proves shipped removal, voluntary-leave-as-removal, dissolve, local-delete, re-invite, first-class ban/unban, and remote delete tombstone replay paths after `PREREQ-REMOTE-EVENT-FAMILIES` added the missing trusted-private system event models and replay matrix.
- EC-007 is now recorded as `Covered`: current repo evidence proves local stale role/invite rechecks, receive-side stale mutation rejection, invalid signed-snapshot invite rejection, and `PREREQ-INVITER-FRESHNESS` proof for stale self-consistent signed invite rejection before pending/group/key/join/mailbox/notification/consumption side effects.
- Rows still `Open` or `Partial` are kept unresolved as `implementation-ready` or `evidence-gated`; none are downgraded into acceptance-only or doc-only cleanup.
- Rows requiring true PubSub forwarding proof, identity/key binding proof, raw protocol injection, relay behavior, packet-capture/privacy proof, or device-lab evidence stay `evidence-gated` until that proof exists.
- TP-SMOKE rows in the source file are supporting smoke scenarios, not source matrix rows. They are included only as likely named gates where they cover a retained row.

## Shared Prerequisites

- No new shared prerequisite session was added.
- Rows do not depend on one another by default.
- Operational prerequisites noted inside row entries include configured `FLUTTER_DEVICE_ID`, configured `MKNOON_RELAY_ADDRESSES`, paired simulator/device availability, Go raw-envelope/security harness availability, relay/CLI peer fixtures, OS notification permissions, and packet-capture/privacy proof tooling.
- Those operational prerequisites do not replace row ownership; each source row must still close through its own session id and source matrix update.
- EK-003 no longer records `missing_first_class_device_identity_model`: `PREREQ-DEVICE-IDENTITY` added first-class device roster fields and valid-device versus invalid-device production proof. Per-device compromise recovery and full welcome/key-package validation remain separate EK-008/EK-011 scope.
- EK-004 no longer records `missing_complete_offline_replay_signature_equivalence`: signed replay envelopes, fail-closed invalid/unsigned replay handling, history repair replay verification, pending-key repair replay verification, and all-family preservation evidence are implemented and accepted.
- EK-005 no longer records `missing_future_epoch_queue_repair_primitives`: `PREREQ-FUTURE-EPOCH-KEY-REPAIR` added durable queueing, scoped repair trigger, retry after key arrival, safe placeholder replacement/finalization, and green direct/named-gate evidence.
- EK-011 no longer records the first-class welcome/key-package blockers: `PREREQ-WELCOME-KEY-PACKAGE` added the model, signed payload binding, validation matrix, durable tombstones, and production local package-id wiring with green final QA evidence. The prerequisite is accepted/qa_passed.
- EK-012 no longer records replay-family blockers after `PREREQ-REMOTE-EVENT-FAMILIES`: shipped message/invite replay, system-transition signed replay, future/missing-key repair replay, key-package replay/tombstones, and trusted-private ban/unban/delete replay diagnostics are covered.
- OS-006 no longer records the history-gap blocker set after `PREREQ-HISTORY-GAP-REPAIR`: the direct/multi-source repair primitive, durable lifecycle state, production repair-range seam, repair-clearance proof, source-doc evidence, and final QA acceptance exist.
- DB-004 no longer records durable group sync cursor, receipt owner, or transaction-boundary blockers after `PREREQ-GROUP-SYNC-RECEIPTS`: migration/helper/repository/drain/listener implementation and direct rollback/idempotency proof close the row.
- DB-006 prerequisite blockers are resolved by `PREREQ-SECRET-STORAGE-WRAPPING`: media attachment keys and group key material now have a primary secure-storage owner, ordinary SQL contains non-secret references, startup legacy scrub removes plaintext-equivalent rows, and final QA accepted the focused tests/gates.
- DB-012 no longer records row-family idempotency blockers after `PREREQ-REMOTE-EVENT-FAMILIES`: row-named remote event types now have production apply/tombstone paths and duplicate/conflicting replay proof.
- ER-004 no longer records the live placeholder, key-sync trigger, durable future-epoch queue, or repair-finalization blockers: `PREREQ-FUTURE-EPOCH-KEY-REPAIR` added those repair lifecycle primitives with green direct/named-gate evidence.
- EC-006 no longer records tombstone-family blockers after `PREREQ-REMOTE-EVENT-FAMILIES`: shipped removal/dissolve/local-delete/re-invite plus trusted-private ban/unban/remote-delete tombstones have concrete replay proof.
- EC-007 no longer records inviter-freshness blockers after `PREREQ-INVITER-FRESHNESS`: signed invite membership freshness proof, sender-side current repository recheck, receive/listener/accept stale-proof rejection, and offline fake-network replay proof are implemented and QA-accepted.

| EC-003 | Future-dated or future-epoch events queue, expire, or reject safely | P0 | Covered | Edge Cases, Invalid Actions, and Fork Handling | needs_repo_evidence | EC-003 |
| EC-004 | Old but valid events apply only if they do not conflict with finalized newer state | P0 | Covered | Edge Cases, Invalid Actions, and Fork Handling | needs_repo_evidence | EC-004 |

| EC-007 | Role change after demotion and invite after removal are rejected across offline replay | P0 | Covered | Edge Cases, Invalid Actions, and Fork Handling | accepted | PREREQ-INVITER-FRESHNESS |

## Row Traceability Rule

- Every source row maps to exactly one session id in this artifact.
- No source row maps to `duplicate_of`; the retained matrix has no duplicate Test IDs.
- Session ids preserve source row ids verbatim because every source row id is filename-safe.
- Later closure work must report final truth per source row, not only per broad subsystem, smoke suite, or rollout residual.
- TP-SMOKE rows are not source rows and must not be counted as sessions unless a later matrix explicitly promotes them into source rows.

## Ordered Session Breakdown

Default order is explicit shared prerequisite sessions, then P0 rows in source order, then P1 rows, then P2 rows. The initial 49 row-owned entries remain in source order to preserve closure evidence. The 2026-05-01 reconciliation created/reopened the shared prerequisite sessions listed after the row-owned table; those prerequisite sessions are the next repo-owned work surfaces and do not move any source row to `Covered` by themselves.

| order | session id | source row id | scenario title | source status | row disposition | classification | intended plan file | exact scope | owns | likely code-entry files | likely direct tests or regressions | likely named gates | dependency on earlier sessions | matrix or closure docs to update |

## Downstream Execution Path

1. For the next row or prerequisite to plan, create the doc-scoped plan file named in the session ledger: `trusted_private_libp2p_group_chat_missing_test_matrix_full_with_rules-session-<SESSION-ID>-plan.md`.
2. Use the ordered-session or reopened-prerequisite entry as the scope contract. Do not merge it with adjacent rows unless the strict row merge rule is explicitly rechecked and still preserves exact row traceability.
3. Execute sessions through the normal implementation planning/execution/closure pipeline when requested. Evidence-gated rows should collect the named proof first, then patch only observed row-owned gaps.
4. A source row is not closed until the source matrix row is updated from `Open` or `Partial` to `Covered` or `Closed` with concrete evidence: files, direct commands, gate outcomes, and any unresolved caveats.
5. After a source row closes, update this breakdown ledger/ordered entry and `Test-Flight-Improv/Group-Chat-Feature/test-inventory.md` only with evidence from that row-owned or prerequisite-owner session.
